# Special Edition Books – 2022 Publications

[Collecting](https://beautifulbooks.info/illustratedbibliographies/)  »  [Articles](https://beautifulbooks.info/articles/)  »  [Special Editions](https://beautifulbooks.info/finding-fancy-books/special-editions/)  »  2022 Archives

## Special Editions Released in 2022

**This page is provided for archive purposes.**

##### ✫ [Upcoming special editions are available here…](https://beautifulbooks.info/finding-fancy-books/special-editions/) ✫

* * *

This page is an archive of “special editions” published in 2022 – a couple are OOP but most are still available to buy, so please enjoy perusing the titles!

Jump to release date:

I deeply appreciate your support of my site if you use these links, but warmly encourage you to buy from your local Indie bookshop if you have the opportunity._

#### December 2022

[![st claire queen of myth WS](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20188%20300'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/st-claire-queen-of-myth-WS.jpg)

[![Special Edition Books - 2022 Publications](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20191%20300'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/st-clair-queen-of-myth-BN.jpg)

##### **Queen of Myth and Monsters** (Adrian X Isolde) by Scarlett St Clair

Dec 27, 2022

Fantasy. Isolde's love for the vampire Adrian each other has cost Isolde her father and her homeland. With two opposing goddesses playing mortals and vampires like chess pieces against one another, Isolde is uncertain who her allies are in the vampire stronghold of Revekka.

**_Waterstones exclusive_**: UK paperback with exclusive cover colourway, a sprayed edge, an extra chapter and a graphic novel short story.

➤ **Find it at** [**Waterstones**](https://tidd.ly/3N1xpWK)

* * *

**_B&N exclusive_**: US paperback with bonus chapter of Adrian and Isolde during the winter holidays, as well as an eight-page graphic novel interstitial of Adrian's chapter of King of Battle and Blood.

➤ **Find it at** [**Barnes & Noble**](https://www.anrdoezrs.net/click-100208466-12366831?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.barnesandnoble.com%2Fw%2Fqueen-of-myth-and-monsters-scarlett-st-clair%2F1140977820%3Fean%3D9781728267500)

* * *

[![osman-bullet-that-missed-WS-spredges](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20182%20300'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/osman-bullet-that-missed-WS-spredges.jpg)

##### **The Bullet that Missed** (Thursday Murder Club) by Richard Osman

Dec 19, 2022

Osman's beloved ageing investigators return in another captivating mystery that blends wry wit and deft characterisation with fast-paced, intricate plotting.

**_Dymocks exclusive_**: hardback with a fox stencilled edge plus an extra short story adventure with the beloved Shiraz-swilling, cake-making, cardigan-wearing Joyce.

➤ **Find it at [Dymocks (Australia)](https://www.dymocks.com.au/book/the-bullet-that-missed-exclusive-edition-by-richard-osman-9780241630693)** nb: seems to be the same as the UK [**Waterstones exclusive edition**](https://tidd.ly/3IkDs9U)

* * *

[![liu monstress 2 BN](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20195%20300'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/liu-monstress-2-BN.webp)

##### **Monstress Book Two** by Marjorie Liu and Sana Takeda

Dec 13, 2022

Graphic novel. A teenage girl struggles to overcome the trauma of war, a task that's made all the more difficult by her mysterious psychic link to an eldritch monster of tremendous power.

**_B&N exclusive_**: signed by Marjorie Liu and will include an exclusive cover and postcards featuring the artwork of series' artist Sana Takeda.

➤ **Find it at** [**Barnes & Noble**](https://www.kqzyfj.com/click-100208466-12366831?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.barnesandnoble.com%2Fw%2Fmonstress-book-two-marjorie-liu%2F1140949688%3Fean%3D9781534325319)

##### **Wordsworth Luxe Collection** by various authors

Dec 15, 2022.

A new limited ‘deluxe' collection of classics by Wordsworth publishing, with a hand-etched design with foil detail embossed on a linen cover, sprayed page edges, patterned end-papers and a silk ribbon marker.

**_Titles include_**

- _Little Women_ by Louisa May Alcott
- _Pride and Prejudice_ by Jane Austen
- _Jane Eyre_ by Charlotte Brontë
- _Wuthering Heights_ by Emily Brontë
- _The Great Gatsby_ by F. Scott Fitzgerald
- _Anne of Green Gables_ by Lucy Montgomery

☞ [Learn more about Wordsworth Classics…](https://beautifulbooks.info/2018/10/wordsworths-collectors-editions-of-classic-childrens-novels/)

➤ **Find the Luxe Collection at [Amazon](https://amzn.to/3PYv0z4) \|** [**Book** **Depository**](https://tidd.ly/3GozdZu)

[![liu monstress 2 BN](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20195%20300'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/liu-monstress-2-BN.webp)

##### **Monstress Book Two** by Marjorie Liu and Sana Takeda

Dec 13, 2022

Graphic novel. A teenage girl struggles to overcome the trauma of war, a task that's made all the more difficult by her mysterious psychic link to an eldritch monster of tremendous power.

**_B&N exclusive_**: signed by Marjorie Liu and will include an exclusive cover and postcards featuring the artwork of series' artist Sana Takeda.

➤ **Find it at** [**Barnes & Noble**](https://www.kqzyfj.com/click-100208466-12366831?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.barnesandnoble.com%2Fw%2Fmonstress-book-two-marjorie-liu%2F1140949688%3Fean%3D9781534325319)

[![jordan eye of the worlds CE orbit](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20189%20300'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/jordan-eye-of-the-worlds-CE-orbit.jpg)

##### **The Eye of the World** (Wheel of Time \#1) by Robert Jordan

Dec 8, 2022.

Classic fantasy.

When their village is attacked by terrifying creatures, Rand al'Thor and his friends are forced to flee for their lives. An ancient evil is stirring, and its servants are scouring the land for the Dragon Reborn – the prophesised hero who can deliver the world from darkness. In this Age of myth and legend, the Wheel of Time turns. What was, what may be, and what is, may yet fall under the Shadow.

**_Collector's Edition_**: UK hardback with gold-foiled illustration on the front cover, exclusive gold-foil illustrations on both sides of the slipcase, an exclusive new Two Rivers illustration as front endpapers, the classic Wheel of Time world map as back endpapers, an exclusive foreword from international bestselling fantasy author Brent Weeks, plus sprayed edges, head and tail bands and a gold ribbon marker. Limited to 1000 copies.

➤ **Find at [Orbit](https://store.orbit-books.co.uk/products/the-eye-of-the-world-deluxe-collectors-edition) \| [Abes](https://affiliates.abebooks.com/c/1223186/77416/2029?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.abebooks.com%2Fservlet%2FSearchResults%3Fbi%3D0%26bx%3Doff%26cm_sp%3DSearchF-_-Advs-_-Result%26ds%3D30%26isbn%3D9780356519470%26recentlyadded%3Dall%26rollup%3Don%26sortby%3D20%26sts%3Dt%26xdesc%3Doff%26xpod%3Doff) \| [eBay](https://ebay.us/3wXvqs)**

[![hessel story of art BN](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20203%20300'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2023/04/hessel-story-of-art-BN.webp)

##### **The Story of Art Without Men** by Katy Hessel

Dec 8, 2022.

A revisionist history of art that turns the limelight on female creativity and the way it has shaped and enriched our world.

**_Waterstones Exclusive_**: UK hardback signed by the author with slipcase.

➤ **Find at [Waterstones](https://tidd.ly/3jy901T)**

**_B&N Exclusive_**: US hardback signed by the author with a 5×7 color reproduction of 17th Century Dutch Artist Rachel Ruysch’s “Still Life With Flowers on a Marble Tabletop,” which Hessel discusses in the book..

➤ **Find at [Barnes & Noble](https://www.kqzyfj.com/click-100208466-12366831?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.barnesandnoble.com%2Fw%2Fthe-story-of-art-without-men-katy-hessel%2F1141471389%3Fean%3D9781324074311)**

##### **Alone With You In The Ether** by Olivie Blake

Dec 8, 2022.

A beautifully wrought romance about love, mental health and the damage we can inflict on others without meaning to.

**_Waterstones exclusive edition_**: UK hardback with honeycomb stencilled page edges.

➤ **Find at [Waterstones](https://tidd.ly/3GE9Vp1)**

##### **Ninth House** by Leigh Bardugo

Dec 6, 2022.

Multiple homicide, secret societies and some very disturbing occult practices abound in this Yale classroom.

**_Waterstones exclusive_**: UK paperback with exclusive yellow colourway.

➤ **Find it at [Waterstones](https://tidd.ly/3F571dS)**

##### **Sword of Destiny** by Andrzej Sapkowski, translated by David French

Dec 6, 2022.

The second story collection in the bestselling series that inspired the hit Netflix show.

**_Illustrated edition_**: Illustrated special edition by a range of artists.

➤ **Find it at [Amazon](https://amzn.to/3NfkeS0) \| [Book Depository](https://tidd.ly/3blgnFD)**

##### **The Passenger & Stella LE Slipcase** by Cormac McCarthy

Thrillers. A literary duet about the complex relationship between two siblings, Bobby Western and Stella Maris.

**_LE slipcase_**: UK hardbacks in slipcase.

##### **The Prison Healer** \[Australian LE\] by Lynette Noni

Dec 1, 2022

Thrillers. A literary duet about the complex relationship between two siblings, Bobby Western and Stella Maris.

**_Limited Edition_**: Exclusive luxe hardback edition with full colour character art work, two-colour printing on chapter headers and maps, a personal letter and other bonus content from the author, metallic sheen dust jacket and lock design on the case underneath.

➤ **Find it at [Booktopia](https://www.booktopia.com.au/the-prison-healer-limited-collector-s-edition-lynette-noni/book/9781761340284.html)**

Nov 29, 2022.

A richly illustrated and romantic origin story of Mary E. Pearson's Remnant universe, the world of _Dance of Thieves_, _Vow of Thieves_ and the New York Times-bestselling Remnant Chronicles.

##### **Seven Husbands of Evelyn Hugo** by Taylor Jenkins Reid

Nov 24, 2022

An iconic Hollywood star mysteriously chooses an unknown young journalist to chronicle her life story in this sumptuous tale of ambition, regret and forbidden love.

**_Waterstones exclusive_**: UK hardback edition with gold foiling and additional author letter.

➤ **Find it at** [**Waterstones**](https://tidd.ly/3ES1BmI)

##### **Snow White and other Grimm's Fairy Tales \[Interactive Edition\]** by MinaLima

Nov 24, 2022

Children's. An illustrated collection of 23 Grimm's fairy tales with interactive features.

☞ Read more about the **[MinaLima Interactive Children's Classics](https://beautifulbooks.info/minalima/)** series.

**_Interactive edition_**: Includes nine interactive features ranging from a pop-up forest and pull-tab mirror for Snow White and a wall of thorns encasing Sleeping Beauty to a three-dimensional ball gown for Cinderella and a pop-up tower for Rapunzel.

##### **A Message from Ukraine** by Volodymyr Zelensky

Nov 24, 2022

Brings together President Volodymyr Zelensky's powerful war speeches that reflect on his nation defending itself from Russian aggression and fighting for the values of the democratic world.

**_Waterstones exclusive_**: Includes an extra speech from President Zelensky and a speech from Olena Volodymyrivna Zelenska, First Lady of Ukraine.

➤ **Find it at** [**Waterstones**](https://tidd.ly/3g7H8jg)

##### **Snow Crash** by Neal Stephenson

Nov 22, 2022.

Deluxe edition of the modern classic that predicted the metaverse. Hiro lives in a Los Angeles where franchises line the freeway as far as the eye can see. The only relief from the sea of logos is within the autonomous city-states, where law-abiding citizens don’t dare leave their mansions. He spends most of his time goggled in to the Metaverse, where his avatar is legendary.

**_Deluxe edition_**: US hardback with new material and decorative endpapers.

➤ **Find at [Amazon](https://amzn.to/3GS9o53) \| [Book Depository](https://tidd.ly/3Ewt5MQ)**

Nov 22, 2022.

A retelling of the legend of Achilles and the Trojan War.

[![steadman skandar WS autumn](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20300%20240'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/steadman-skandar-WS-autumn.jpg)

##### **Skandar and the Unicorn Thief** by A. F. Steadman

Nov 17, 2022.

A magical world full of courageous heroes and warrior unicorns in the first instalment of Steadman's series, as young Skandar takes to the skies to battle a deadly enemy.

**Waterstones “Autumn” Exclusive:** Replacing the initial exclusive edition, this new special edition has sprayed edges, gold foil pattern, prologue of book two, note from the author and bonus information on the fire element.

➤ **Find it at [Waterstones](https://tidd.ly/3UXk06U)**

**➤ Find signed exclusive at [Waterstones](https://tidd.ly/3VeQSrv)**

* * *

[![berger book dictionary](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20210%20300'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/berger-book-dictionary.jpg)

##### **The Dictionary of the Book** by Sidney E. Berger

Nov 15, 2022.

The definitive glossary of the book covers all the terms needed for a thorough understanding of how books are made, the materials they are made of, and how they are described in the bookselling, book collecting, and library worlds.

➤ **Find it at [Amazon](https://amzn.to/3PkLOOS) \| [Book Depository](https://tidd.ly/3C0v0JL)**

* * *

[![wharton custom country vitae](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20195%20300'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/wharton-custom-country-vitae.jpg)

##### **The Silmarillion** by J. R. R. Tolkien

Nov 10, 2022

A special edition of the forerunner to The Lord of the Rings, illustrated throughout in colour by J.R.R. Tolkien himself and with the complete text printed in two colours.

**_Illustrated edition_**: Hardback, with stencilled green page edges, Tolkien's own paintings and drawings for the first time, two colour printing, and a letter written by Tolkien in 1951 which provides a brilliant exposition of the earlier Ages.

Collector's note: A companion to the matching [_Lord of the Rings_ edition released last year](https://beautifulbooks.info/finding-fancy-books/special-editions/?elementor-preview=113468&ver=1656129363#lotr).

➤ **Find it at** **[Amazon](https://amzn.to/36UxBYs) \| [Book Depository](https://tidd.ly/3wFcsvZ)**

* * *

**_Limited edition_**: Hardback in a slipcase, quarter-bound with blue leather, including Tolkien's own paintings and drawings for the first time, two colour printing, and a letter written by Tolkien in 1951 which provides a brilliant exposition of the earlier Ages. Unique to this edition are two poster-size, fold-out maps revealing all the detail of Beleriand as the tales grew, an illustrated booklet featuring ‘A Brief Account of The Silmarillion and its Making’ by Christopher Tolkien, and a printed art card reproducing ‘Taniquetil’.

Collector's note: A companion to the matching [_Lord of the Rings_ limited edition released last year](https://beautifulbooks.info/finding-fancy-books/special-editions/special-editions-2022-archives/#LOTRLE).

➤ **Find it at** **[Amazon](https://amzn.to/3NaP4LK) \| [Book Depository](https://tidd.ly/3A08Pm8)**

##### **Akira: Art of Wall** by Katsuhiro Otomo

Jun 7, 2022.

Manga. Akira author Katsuhiro Otomo worked with artist Kosuke Kawamura to enrobe a Tokyo city block in a collage of gripping moments from the manga that revolutionized an art form. **_Collector's edition_**: Silver foil-coated collector's box presents an exquisite reproduction of Otomo and Kawamura's work, with nearly 75 feet of illustrations in three accordion-bound volumes. A fourth volume includes an exclusive interview with Otomo and Kawamura, as well as photographs of the original exhibition. Rounding out the box is a dramatic, 16.5×23.4-inch poster.

Speculative fiction. A chronicle of love, the meaning of family and the excruciating cost of unattainable dreams, traversing three centuries and three alternative versions of America.\
\
**_Waterstones exclusive_**: Signed UK hardback. Includes exclusive author Q&A.\
\
➤ **Find it at** [**Waterstones**](https://tidd.ly/3AhknhN)\

\
##### **Detransition, Baby** – Torrey Peters\
\
Jan 6, 2022.\
\
Fiction. Juliet Jacques Reese nearly had it all: a loving relationship with Amy, an apartment in New York, a job she didn't hate. She'd scraped together a life previous generations of trans women could only dream of; the only thing missing was a child. Then everything fell apart and three years on Reese is still in self-destruct mode, avoiding her loneliness by sleeping with married men. When her ex calls to ask if she wants to be a mother, Reese finds herself intrigued. After being attacked in the street, Amy de-transitioned to become Ames, changed jobs and, thinking he was infertile, started an affair with his boss Katrina. Now Katrina's pregnant.\
\
**_Waterstones exclusive_**: UK paperback with red sprayed page edges.\
\
➤ **Find it at** [**Waterstones**](https://tidd.ly/3noGii2)\
\

[![may-wahala-waterstones](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20220%20300'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/may-wahala-waterstones.jpg)\
\
##### **Wahala** – Nikki May\
\
Jan 6, 2022.\
\
Fiction. Ronke, Simi, Boo are three mixed-race friends living in London. They have the gift of two cultures, Nigerian and English, though not all of them choose to see it that way. Everyday racism has never held them back, but now in their thirties, they question their future. Ronke wants a husband (he must be Nigerian); Boo enjoys (correction: endures) stay-at-home motherhood; while Simi, full of fashion career dreams, rolls her eyes as her boss refers to her urban vibe yet again. When Isobel, a lethally glamorous friend from their past arrives in town, she is determined to fix their futures for them.\
\
**_Waterstones exclusive_**: UK hardback with exclusive pink edges, recipe content and designed endpapers.\
\
➤ **Find it at** [**Waterstones**](https://tidd.ly/3nfbbWg)\
\

##### **When I Was Ten** – Fiona Cummins\

Jan 6, 2022.\
\
Crime. Twenty-one years ago, Dr Richard Carter and his wife Pamela were killed in what has become the most infamous double murder of the modern age. Their ten year-old daughter – nicknamed the Angel of Death – spent eight years in a children's secure unit and is living quietly under an assumed name with a family of her own. Now, on the anniversary of the trial, a documentary team has tracked down her older sister, compelling her to break two decades of silence.\
\
**_Waterstones exclusive_**: Signed UK paperback with scissor stencilled page edges.\
